&#39;=================== More Information Below =================&#39;

<b> ðŸŽ² SHONEN ROLL ðŸŽ²</b>

<b>Momentum:</b>
Whenever a shinobi moment succeeds, the user can roll again on their next turn to continue the action until they fail. This will also lower the required roll by 1 everytime it succeeds!(This can only be used on SHinobi Flash)

<b>Survival Instinct:</b>
A Shonen Roll can be used to survive an otherwise lethal attack, allowing the player to either escape to fight another day or endure and continue battling. This requires a roll of 10 or higher. Any death resulting from a Shonen Roll failure has a 100% death rate.

<b>Fighting Spirit:</b>
A Shonen Roll can be used to empower a technique, increasing its speed and power by one step. This requires a roll of 10 or higher.
